10a7(1): po zas gtsang ma ri nga'i bral nga la ba'am/ bsnyed bkur bya ba'i byingasu yang ma 'gro shig/ lal zhig de bral paba'am/ bskod bkur bya ba 'byir so na/ lus la ban

10b4(1): la shang na la bdun srid du 'phags te/ rdzu 'phrul gyos par snang ba skyil mo dkrung bcas shing / 'ong ba mthong nas/ de la thal mo sbyar totshogs su bcang nas smras pa/ tshod bsgyur mos

11a1(1): zil gyis gnang pa'i mu stegs gzhan mi snga ji ltar nyi ma'i zil gnod rdza ni/ nam mkha'i dbyings na 'od sosror nyin mi snang/ de bzhin khyod

11b5(1): mtsho bsten par bya/ tshul khrims rnam dag rtsa brtan par bzug/ ting 'dzin lom dran pa mala'adang / byang chub yan lag me dog stong pa'i sdong / bdag beng grib ljar rgyal ba'i srong
11b6(1): sden/ tshul khrims nags mtha' sten pa'i stobs chen po/ ting 'dzin zhi ba'i ri khror phug ra gnas/ stong pa mtshan med spyod med spyod yul can/ rgyal ba stobs can seng ge khyod kyis sras/ 
11b7(1): thub pa mi gnas gnas ni rnam par stod/ rgyal ba khyu mchog brjid pa'i stabs bzhug pas/ byis pa so so mu stegs gzhan spangs te/ khyod kyi sras ni khyu mchog sgra yang 'byin/ tshul
11b8(1): khrims gter dang yon tan dbyig gis brgyad/ bsam gtad dang ba'i zhi gnas nye bar bskyabs/ ye shes kyis bsrungs thar pa'i spyod yul can/ rgyal ba tshong dpon gtso bo nor gtong
11b9(1): mdzad/ dge ba yongs su bzung ba'i sdig bcom ste/ nyon mongs zhi mdzad dge sten dga' sogs pas/ lha dang lha min bcas pa'i 'jig rten na/ rgyal po khyod kyi sras mchog rnam

12b8(1): 'dug ni su'i yis bsrungs/ 'char kas sbas pa/ byams pa'i stobs kyis/ thub pa yongs bsrungs te/ de'i dpung ye shes nyan thos zhab ring g.yo ga/ yon tan tshogs la
